        INNER JOIN [Permissions] AS [p] ON [f].[Id] = [p].[FunctionId]
        INNER JOIN [AppRoles] AS [r] ON [p].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
        WHERE ([r].[Name] IN (N'Admin') AND ([f].[Id] = @__functionId_1)) AND ([p].[CanRead] = 1))
    THEN CAST(1 AS BIT) ELSE CAST(0 AS BIT)
END" (0723d8ff)

        FROM [Functions] AS [f]
        INNER JOIN [Permissions] AS [p] ON [f].[Id] = [p].[FunctionId]

END" (0723d8ff)
